m-sꜣ tꜣ nẖb.t n nꜣ pr-ꜥꜣ.w ꞽw =f hꜥy ḥr s.t-mnṱ sḥm.t ꞽw =s ḏqm =s n.ꞽm =s nꜣ.w-ꜥn =s ꞽw =s ꜥš ꞽmn r ḥꜣty =s nḏm ꞽw =w (r) ṯꜣy nkt mtw =s mtw =s lky =s mtw =s ꞽr yꜥby wḥmy.t pꜣ mnq pꜣ ḏmꜥ ḥnṱs ḏd-md.t nṯr-ḥr =k ḥsmn nb-špꜣ-nṯr.t mtw =n ḥwy qrr r.r =w wp-st pꜣ-šr-ḫnsw r-ẖ pꜣ 2/3 ẖnm-pꜣ-rꜥ r-ẖ pꜣ 1/3 n tꜣ dny.t 5.t nty-ḥry pꜣy =w wn dmḏ my dy =w s pꜣ rmṯ nty-ꞽw =f (r) ꞽy r.ḥr =tn n-rn tꜣ-šr.t-hry=w ꞽrm pꜣ-ꞽwꞽw-ḥr mtw =y dy.t wꜥb =w ꞽ.ꞽr-ḥr pꜣ-dy-wsꞽr sꜣ pa-ꞽmn pꜣy =(y) šr n-ḏr.t ms =w s ꞽn ms =w ḥꜣty =y ꞽrm =f ꞽn ꞽ.ꞽr =w ẖdb (=y) r-ḏbꜣ pꜣy =(y) šr nḥm =k pr-ꜥꜣ m-ꜥw tmy nb tꜣ r wꜥb =s n pꜣy =s hy (n) gtgt r rd.ṱ =s pẖr.t (n) sḥm.t n ḥwe =s (r) ẖe.t =s n tꜣy =s ꜣty.t qš ḥwy n =s wꜥ n.ꞽm =w ꞽn-ḥꜣ =s kꞽꞽ ꞽ:ꞽr-ḥr =s wꜥb ḥq wꜥb =y ḏd-md.t ꜥnḫ =k rpy =k rpy by =k m grḥ m hrw m nw nb r nḥḥ ḫꜣꜥ r pꜣy =s ꜥ.wꞽ sẖ sy-sbk sꜣ pꜣ-šr-mn r-ḫrw tꜣ-šr.t-pꜣ-mr-iḥ sẖ sy-sbk sꜣ wn-nfr r-ḫrw =w ḏꜣḏꜣ =s n ꞽrp r ḏi̯.t ḥs n ꞽꜥꜣ r šy sḫfy sḥm.t n tꜣꞽ ḥty ꞽw =y wꜥb.k sẖ pꜣ-šr-mn sꜣ wn-nfr r-ḫrw tꜣ-šr.t-mn ḏi̯.t ḥbs ꞽw =f km ꞽ:ꞽri̯ =f n =s (n) ḥwy pꜣ-dy-ḥr ꞽrm nꜣy =f sn(.w) sm(ꜣꜥ) r wn-nfr mḥ wsꞽr šꜥ ḏ.t wꜥb rꜣ =y ḫꜣꜥ =f ḥr tꜣ ḏꜣy(.t) wbꜣ =s pẖr.t (r) ḏi̯.t r:ꜥḥꜥ msi̯ r sḥm.t ꞽw.ꞽ(w) =s ꜥšꜣ wꜥb =y kt n wꜥ sp ḏi̯.t (n) nꜣy =s ꞽwf.w st šsp-n-ꞽp ṯꜣy n =k mw ḥr tꜣ ḥtp.t m-sꜣ wsꞽr r-ḫrw ꜣs.t tꜣ nṯr.t-ꜥꜣ.t sẖ wn-nfr sꜣ pꜣ-šr-mn r-ḫrw tꜣ-šr.t-ꞽy-m-ḥtp nꜣ pẖr.w(t) mtw =w r.ꞽri̯ =w r ḏi̯.t sḫfy r sḥm.t kt ḏrꜣ.t bty ꞽbe(.t) nḥḥ r tꜣ wnw.t n-rn =s tꜣ-šr.t-mw.t tꜣy pꜣ-tw-ḫnsw sꜣ pꜣ-dy-ḥr ḥtp-nsw ḏd-md.t snṱ =tw-tn wy ḥtp-nsw ꜣṱy.n =f pr ꞽṱ =f wsꞽr rꜣ n ṯꜣy sd ꞽw =y wꜥb.k ꞽw =y (r) dy.t ꞽr s ta-spd ta krrws ḏd sḥm.t ta-spd ta grrws mw.t =s sms.t n sḥm.t ta-sty ta ḥr-wn-nfr mw.t =s ꜣs.t-wr(y) ꞽw =y (r) ꞽr =w n sḥm.t tꜣy-gꜣ ta pa-tꜣ.wy sẖ ꞽry-ꜥꜣ-(n-)ꞽmn ꞽy-m-ḥtp sꜣ ꞽmn-ḥtp ꞽr =t n =y pꜣy =w hp tꜣy =w wpy pꜣy =w ꜥnḫ m-bꜣḥ ẖnm mtw =y ꞽr =w r-ḫrw =f n ḥtr ꞽwty mn ꞽwty sh̭ nb dy nꜣ wpṱy.w mꜣꜥ r.ḥr =y n.ꞽm =w mn-mtw =y md(.t) nb n pꜣ tꜣ ꞽ.ꞽr-n =t n-rn =w n-ṯꜣy pꜣ-hrw r-ḥry rnp.t nb šꜥ ḏ.t
